## Section 2 — Skipped Names (Not in New System)

These old max names have no equivalent in the new system and will be skipped during import:

- 5RM Barbell Row
- Bulgarian Split Squat
- Floor Press
- Good Morning
- Hip Bridge
- Pause Bench Press
- Thrusters/Barbell Row Time
